## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration in such systems typically arises from restoring forces (functions of x) and damping forces (functions of v), potentially with nonlinear terms like cubic restoring forces (Duffing oscillator) or nonlinear damping (van der Pol oscillator).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic restoring force: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear spring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (1 + c2 * x**2) (nonlinear damping depending on position)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * x**2 + c2 * v (position-dependent damping)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Cubic damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (nonlinear velocity-dependent dissipation)
- Forced nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (periodic external driving)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) (time-varying stiffness)
- Mixed nonlinear terms: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * v * x**2 (Duffing + van der Pol combined)
- Softening spring with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**2 + c3 * v (general polynomial restoring force + damping)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force approximation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear restoring force (simple harmonic motion) → term proportional to -x (negative coefficient for stability)
- Cubic position dependence → Duffing-type nonlinearity x**3 indicating hardening or softening spring
- Velocity-position coupling v*x**2 → van der Pol type nonlinear damping / self-excitation mechanism
- Odd-power position terms (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric restoring force about equilibrium
- Even-power position terms (x**2) → asymmetric potential / broken symmetry in oscillator
- Odd-power velocity terms (v, v**3) → dissipative forces preserving time-reversal antisymmetry
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) → external periodic forcing or parametric excitation
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous system where phase portrait fully characterizes dynamics
- Product of velocity and position powers → energy-dependent damping characteristic of limit cycle oscillators
- Ratio of acceleration to position giving non-constant value → signature of nonlinear frequency-amplitude dependence

- Linear in v: coefficient ≈ -0.5995
- Contains `x*exp(-|x|)` which is NOT a polynomial, NOT a simple exponential, NOT a trig function
- `x*exp(-|x|)` behaves differently for x>0 (`x*exp(-x)`) and x<0 (`x*exp(x)`)

**Candidate 64: c0*x + c1*v + c2*x*log(c3*x**2 + 1)**
`x*log(c3*x²+1)` ≠ `x*exp(-|x|)`. No match.
